SURNAME INDEX TO THE ALBUQUERQUE JOURNAL -1937 


INTRODUCTION 

The idea for this index first came about as a result of Ms. Drew’s work at the Denver 
Public Library Genealogy Division. That library had certain indexes and materials which 
are invaluable to genealogical researchers. Our new library had a fair amount to offer 
researchers; however, there was little for those who were researching their local “roots”. 
There were few genealogical publications of regional interest. With the publication of 
these indexes that is now beginning to change. 

On her return to the Albuquerque Public Library Special Collections Branch, Ms. Drew 
considered what information would be most useful to those people doing local research. 
One of the best sources of genealogical information is, of course, the local newspaper, but 
there is rarely an index to those records. Therefore, she decided to create one. She 
directed the compilation of the vital statistics for 1925 to 1936, which is available in the 
library, but no extra copies were made for distribution at this time. Under her direction, 
the Albuquerque Genealogy Club undertook the project of further development of these 
indexes. 

A form was developed to cover the major vital records which normally appear in the 
newspaper - births, deaths, marriages, and anniversaries. This would be an index to the 
principals in the article and would cover only those persons of either New Mexican origin 
or who participated in one of these events in New Mexico. In other words, an accident 
occurring in Texas or New York would be indexed ONLY for those persons of New 
Mexico origin or residence. A marriage of a Coloradoan and Californian, married in New 
Mexico and reported in the newspaper, WOULD be Indexed here. 

The Albuquerque Journal contains a great deal of information about events all over the 
state of New Mexico. Since it is the largest newspaper in the state this index can be 
useful for many events which occurred outside of Albuquerque. Be alert when searching 
as often a subject appeared in more than one article on a page. We attempted to show that 
by using “(x2)” to indicate “two times on that page”. 

At this time, the Albuquerque/Bemalillo County Library System has the Albuquerque 
Morning Journal, Albuquerque Journal, and Albuquerque Tribune available on microfilm 
from approximately 1882 to the present. Some early issues are missing. Photocopies of a 
particular record may be obtained from these microfilm copies at the Main Albuquerque 
Public Library. The Special Collections Branch of the Albuquerque Public Library has 
newspaper microfilm for the territorial years (prior to 1912) only. We are attempting a 
complete surname index of the various Albuquerque newspapers from 1880 to 1925 and a 
vital statistics index of the Albuquerque Journal from 1925 to 1960. Many years are 
completed and will be found itemized on another page of this preface. Commencing 
with 1960 we are compiling the obituaries found in the Albuquerque Journal to the 
present time. 



We hope that you will find this index easy to use and filled with relatives for whom you 
have been searching. 

FORMAT 

The format of this index is quite simple. Names are given alphabetically by surname. It 
is compiled on an annual basis. This does mean that users will need to check each year, 
ESPECIALLY if some event occurred towards the latter months of the year. The legend 
is followed by the date and page or pages on which an article appeared. REMEMBER: 
the date shown is the date reported in the newspaper and not necessarily the date of the 
indexed event. 

LEGEND 

B = Birth 

M = Marriage 

D = Death 

P = Probate action 

AB = Anniversary of birth 
AD = Anniversary of death 
AM = Anniversary of marriage 
Div = Divorce action 
(X2) = Two items on the page 


HAPPY SEARCHING 

Laurel E. Drew, Editor 

Hugh Bivens, Compiler 
Howard W. Henry, Project Coordinator 
Eldon W. Pierce, Technical Director 
Fall, 1996. 



PUBLICATIONS 

Albuquerque, New Mexico, Daily Citizen Newspaper: Surname Index for the Year: 

1888 with 5098 entries 197 pages 

1889 with 7616 entries 293 pages 

1890 with 10085 entries 388 pages 

1891 with 10808 entries 210 pages 

1892 with 11282 entries 226 pages 

Albuquerque, New Mexico, Daily Journal Newspaper: Vital Statistics Index: Births, 
Marriages, Anniversaries, Deaths 

1942 with 3963 entries 153 pages 

1943 with 5812 entries 226 pages 

1944 with 5717 entries 221 pages 
1947 with 6216 entries 249 pages 
1949 with 5863 entries 114 pages 

Guest Register, Historic St. James Hotel, Cimarron, New Mexico; Copy of Original 
Register, indexed, dated August 22, 1881, to 1883, and various dates from 1889, 1902, 
and a few in 1905 and 1946; 839 entries and 124 pages 

St. James Customer Ledger for lodging and purchases: 

Vol. 1, Dec, 1871, to Apr, 1875, 265 pages 140 names 
Vol. 2, 1875, 1880; 200 pages 101 names 
Vol. 3, Jan, 1887 - 1902, 162 pages 87 names 

The Methodist/Episcopal Church History, indexed, containing a history of the church 
from founding in Colfax County, New Mexico, in 1867 forward, and many handwritten 
records of baptisms, marriages, and class records from that area. Some records up to 
1918. 1144 entries and 128 pages 

“From The Top of The Mountain, Pie Town, New Mexico, and Neighbors” by Kathryn 
McKee Roberts. This is an index to that publication. 62 pages 

“A Story of Patrick Henry, American Statesman and Orator and Above All, a Father!” by 
Howard W. Henry. This work traces back to 1100 A.D. and brings the family of Patrick 
Henry up to the mid-1850’s with his children, grandchildren, and many others. 82 pages, 
indexed, and 975 names 

Register of City Hotels, Albuquerque, New Mexico 1893
